Listing of Ray Database QUBIC_TD_NS_DICHROIC_64.ZRD
ZRD Format : Compressed Full Data. Double precision data converted to floating point precision.
Units are Millimeters.
Segment 0 data is at the source point of the ray.
Subsequent segment coordinate data is at the end of the segment.
Intensity, phase, cosine, field, and path to values are prior to reflection,
refraction, splitting, absorbing, or scattering at the end point.
End of segment: X = Terminated, R = Reflected, T = Transmitted, S = Scattered, D = Diffracted, B = Bulk Scattered
Split from parent: G = Ghost, E = Diffracted, F = Scattered
Z = Ray Error (terminated)
Filter: none
